helius
======

There is very little structured metadata to build this page from currently. You should check the [main library docs](/helius/0.2.4/helius/)
, [readme](/crate/helius/0.2.4/)
, or [Cargo.toml](/crate/helius/0.2.4/source/Cargo.toml.orig)
 in case the author documented the features in them.

This version has **3** feature flags, **4** of them enabled by **default**.

### default

*   [native-tls](#native-tls)
     (default)

### native-tls (default)

*   [reqwest](/crate/reqwest/^0.11.22)
    /[native-tls](/crate/reqwest/^0.11.22/features#native-tls)
     (default)
*   [tokio-tungstenite](/crate/tokio-tungstenite/^0.24.0)
    /[native-tls](/crate/tokio-tungstenite/^0.24.0/features#native-tls)
     (default)

### rustls

*   [reqwest](/crate/reqwest/^0.11.22)
    /[rustls-tls](/crate/reqwest/^0.11.22/features#rustls-tls)
    
*   [tokio-tungstenite](/crate/tokio-tungstenite/^0.24.0)
    /[rustls-tls-webpki-roots](/crate/tokio-tungstenite/^0.24.0/features#rustls-tls-webpki-roots)

[helius](../index.html)
::[client](index.html)

Struct HeliusCopy item path
===========================

[Source](../../src/helius/client.rs.html#17-28)

    pub struct Helius {
        pub config: Arc<Config>,
        pub client: Client,
        pub rpc_client: Arc<RpcClient>,
        pub async_rpc_client: Option<Arc<RpcClient>>,
        pub ws_client: Option<Arc<EnhancedWebsocket>>,
    }

Expand description

The `Helius` struct is the main entry point to interacting with the SDK

This client is responsible for setting up the network and configuration settins used to interact with the various provided methods. It also provides methods to access RPC client functionalities. The client ensures thread-safe access to the underlying RPC client

Fields[§](#fields)

-------------------

[§](#structfield.config)
`config: [Arc](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/sync/struct.Arc.html "struct alloc::sync::Arc") <[Config](../config/struct.Config.html "struct helius::config::Config") >`

The configuration which specifies an `api_key`, `cluster`, and the requisite `endpoints`

[§](#structfield.client)
`client: [Client](https://docs.rs/reqwest/0.11.27/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/reqwest/async_impl/client/struct.Client.html "struct reqwest::async_impl::client::Client") `

An HTTP client used for making API requests. The client is reused for all requests made through this instance of `Helius`

[§](#structfield.rpc_client)
`rpc_client: [Arc](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/sync/struct.Arc.html "struct alloc::sync::Arc") <[RpcClient](../rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html "struct helius::rpc_client::RpcClient") >`

A reference-counted RPC client tailored for making requests in a thread-safe manner

[§](#structfield.async_rpc_client)
`async_rpc_client: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option") <[Arc](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/sync/struct.Arc.html "struct alloc::sync::Arc") <[RpcClient](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html "struct solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient") >>`

An optional asynchronous Solana client for async operations

[§](#structfield.ws_client)
`ws_client: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option") <[Arc](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/sync/struct.Arc.html "struct alloc::sync::Arc") <[EnhancedWebsocket](../websocket/struct.EnhancedWebsocket.html "struct helius::websocket::EnhancedWebsocket") >>`

A reference-counted enhanced (geyser) websocket client

Implementations[§](#implementations)

-------------------------------------

### impl [Helius](struct.Helius.html "struct helius::client::Helius")

[Source](../../src/helius/client.rs.html#47-59)

#### pub fn [new](#method.new)
(api\_key: &[str](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.str.html)
, cluster: [Cluster](../types/types/enum.Cluster.html "enum helius::types::types::Cluster")
) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")
<Self>

Creates a new instance of `Helius` configured with a specific API key and a target cluster

##### [§](#arguments)
Arguments

*   `api_key` - The API key required for authenticating the requests made
*   `cluster` - The Solana cluster (Devnet or MainnetBeta) that defines the given network environment

##### [§](#returns)
Returns

An instance of `Helius` if successful. A `HeliusError` is returned if an error occurs during configuration or initialization of the HTTP or RPC client

##### [§](#example)
Example

    use helius::client::Helius;
    use helius::types::Cluster;
    
    let helius = Helius::new("your_api_key", Cluster::Devnet).expect("Failed to create a Helius client");

[Source](../../src/helius/client.rs.html#77-90)

#### pub fn [new\_with\_async\_solana](#method.new_with_async_solana)
(api\_key: &[str](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.str.html)
, cluster: [Cluster](../types/types/enum.Cluster.html "enum helius::types::types::Cluster")
) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")
<Self>

Creates a new instance of `Helius` with an asynchronous Solana client

##### [§](#arguments-1)
Arguments

*   `api_key` - The API key required for authenticating the requests made
*   `cluster` - The Solana cluster (Devnet or MainnetBeta) that defines the given network environment

##### [§](#returns-1)
Returns

An instance of `Helius` if successful. A `HeliusError` is returned if an error occurs during configuration or initialization of the HTTP or RPC client

##### [§](#example-1)
Example

    use helius::Helius;
    use helius::types::Cluster;
    
    let helius = Helius::new_with_async_solana("your_api_key", Cluster::Devnet).expect("Failed to create a Helius client");

[Source](../../src/helius/client.rs.html#103-123)

#### pub async fn [new\_with\_ws\_with\_timeouts](#method.new_with_ws_with_timeouts)
( api\_key: &[str](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.str.html)
, cluster: [Cluster](../types/types/enum.Cluster.html "enum helius::types::types::Cluster")
, ping\_interval\_secs: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
\>, pong\_timeout\_secs: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
\>, ) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")
<Self>

The enhanced websocket is optional, and this method is used to create a new instance of `Helius` with an enhanced websocket client. Upon calling this method, the websocket will connect hence the asynchronous function definition omission from the default `new` method.

##### [§](#arguments-2)
Arguments

*   `api_key` - The API key required for authenticating requests made
*   `cluster` - The Solana cluster (Devnet or MainnetBeta) that defines the given network environment
*   `ping_interval_secs` - Optional duration in seconds between ping messages (defaults to 10 seconds if None)
*   `pong_timeout_secs` - Optional duration in seconds to wait for a pong response before considering the connection dead

##### [§](#returns-2)
Returns

An instance of `Helius` if successful. A `HeliusError` is returned if an error occurs during configuration or initialization of the HTTP, RPC, or WS client

[Source](../../src/helius/client.rs.html#135-137)

#### pub async fn [new\_with\_ws](#method.new_with_ws)
(api\_key: &[str](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.str.html)
, cluster: [Cluster](../types/types/enum.Cluster.html "enum helius::types::types::Cluster")
) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")
<Self>

Creates a new instance of `Helius` with an enhanced websocket client using default timeout settings. This is a convenience method that uses default values of 10 seconds for ping interval and 3 failed pings before considering the connection dead.

##### [§](#arguments-3)
Arguments

*   `api_key` - The API key required for authenticating requests made
*   `cluster` - The Solana cluster (Devnet or MainnetBeta) that defines the given network environment

##### [§](#returns-3)
Returns

An instance of `Helius` if successful. A `HeliusError` is returned if an error occurs during configuration or initialization of the HTTP, RPC, or WS client

[Source](../../src/helius/client.rs.html#143-145)

#### pub async fn [parsed\_transaction\_history](#method.parsed_transaction_history)
( &self, request: [ParsedTransactionHistoryRequest](../types/enhanced_transaction_types/struct.ParsedTransactionHistoryRequest.html "struct helius::types::enhanced_transaction_types::ParsedTransactionHistoryRequest")
, ) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")
<[Vec](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/vec/struct.Vec.html "struct alloc::vec::Vec")
<[EnhancedTransaction](../types/enhanced_transaction_types/struct.EnhancedTransaction.html "struct helius::types::enhanced_transaction_types::EnhancedTransaction")
\>>

Retrieves a parsed transaction history for a specific address

##### [§](#arguments-5)
Arguments

*   `ParsedTransactionHistoryRequest` - A parsed transaction history request, which includes:

*   An address for which a given parsed transaction history will be retrieved
*   An optional `before` parameter that, when provided, fetches the parsed transaction history before the given signature. This is useful for pagination

##### [§](#returns-8)
Returns

A `Result` wrapping a vector of `EnhancedTransaction`s

#### pub async fn [delegate\_collection\_authority](#method.delegate_collection_authority)
( &self, collection\_mint: [Pubkey](https://docs.rs/solana-pubkey/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_pubkey/struct.Pubkey.html "struct solana_pubkey::Pubkey")
, new\_collection\_authority: [Pubkey](https://docs.rs/solana-pubkey/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_pubkey/struct.Pubkey.html "struct solana_pubkey::Pubkey")
, update\_authority\_keypair: &[Keypair](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/signer/keypair/struct.Keypair.html "struct solana_sdk::signer::keypair::Keypair")
, payer\_keypair: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<&[Keypair](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/signer/keypair/struct.Keypair.html "struct solana_sdk::signer::keypair::Keypair")
\>, ) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")
<[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
\>

Delegates collection authority to a new authority for a given collection mint.

##### [§](#arguments-12)
Arguments

*   `collection_mint` - The public key of the collection mint.
*   `new_collection_authority` - The public key of the new authority to delegate to.
*   `update_authority_keypair` - The keypair of the current update authority who is delegating the authority.
*   `payer_keypair` - Optional keypair to pay for the transaction fees. If `None`, `update_authority_keypair` is used as the payer.

##### [§](#returns-14)
Returns

A `Result` containing the transaction `Signature` if successful.

[Source](../../src/helius/mint_api.rs.html#71-92)

#### pub async fn [revoke\_collection\_authority](#method.revoke_collection_authority)
( &self, collection\_mint: [Pubkey](https://docs.rs/solana-pubkey/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_pubkey/struct.Pubkey.html "struct solana_pubkey::Pubkey")
, delegated\_collection\_authority: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[Pubkey](https://docs.rs/solana-pubkey/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_pubkey/struct.Pubkey.html "struct solana_pubkey::Pubkey")
\>, revoke\_authority\_keypair: &[Keypair](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/signer/keypair/struct.Keypair.html "struct solana_sdk::signer::keypair::Keypair")
, payer\_keypair: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<&[Keypair](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/signer/keypair/struct.Keypair.html "struct solana_sdk::signer::keypair::Keypair")
\>, ) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")
<[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
\>

Revokes a delegated collection authority for a given collection mint.

##### [§](#arguments-13)
Arguments

*   `collection_mint` - The public key of the collection mint.
*   `delegated_collection_authority` - Optional public key of the delegated authority to revoke. If `None`, the default mint API authority is used.
*   `revoke_authority_keypair` - The keypair of the authority revoking the delegated authority.
*   `payer_keypair` - Optional keypair to pay for the transaction fees. If `None`, `revoke_authority_keypair` is used as the payer.

##### [§](#returns-15)
Returns

A `Result` containing the transaction `Signature` if successful.

#### pub async fn [send\_and\_confirm\_transaction](#method.send_and_confirm_transaction)
( &self, transaction: &impl [SerializableTransaction](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/rpc_client/trait.SerializableTransaction.html "trait solana_rpc_client::rpc_client::SerializableTransaction")
, send\_transaction\_config: [RpcSendTransactionConfig](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSendTransactionConfig.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSendTransactionConfig")
, last\_valid\_block\_height: [u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
, timeout: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")

\>, ) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")

\>

Sends a transaction and handles its confirmation status

##### [§](#arguments-17)
Arguments

*   `transaction` - The transaction to be sent, which implements `SerializableTransaction`
*   `send_transaction_config` - Configuration options for sending the transaction
*   `last_valid_block_height` - The last block height at which the transaction is valid
*   `timeout` - Optional duration for polling transaction confirmation, defaults to 60 seconds

Returns

The transaction signature, if successful

#### pub async fn [get\_compute\_units\_thread\_safe](#method.get_compute_units_thread_safe)
( &self, instructions: [Vec](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/vec/struct.Vec.html "struct alloc::vec::Vec")
<[Instruction](https://docs.rs/solana-instruction/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_instruction/struct.Instruction.html "struct solana_instruction::Instruction")
\>, payer: [Pubkey](https://docs.rs/solana-pubkey/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_pubkey/struct.Pubkey.html "struct solana_pubkey::Pubkey")
, lookup\_tables: [Vec](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/vec/struct.Vec.html "struct alloc::vec::Vec")
<[AddressLookupTableAccount](https://docs.rs/solana-program/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_program/address_lookup_table/struct.AddressLookupTableAccount.html "struct solana_program::address_lookup_table::AddressLookupTableAccount")
\>, keypairs: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<&\[&[Keypair](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/signer/keypair/struct.Keypair.html "struct solana_sdk::signer::keypair::Keypair")\
\]>, ) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")
<[Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
\>>

##### [§](#arguments-18)
Arguments

*   `instructions` - The transaction instructions
*   `payer` - The public key of the payer

*   `keypairs` - The keypairs for the transaction

##### [§](#returns-21)
Returns

The compute units consumed, or None if unsuccessful

[Source](../../src/helius/optimized_transaction.rs.html#506-659)

#### pub async fn [send\_smart\_transaction\_with\_seeds](#method.send_smart_transaction_with_seeds)
( &self, create\_config: [CreateSmartTransactionSeedConfig](../types/types/struct.CreateSmartTransactionSeedConfig.html "struct helius::types::types::CreateSmartTransactionSeedConfig")
, send\_options: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[RpcSendTransactionConfig](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSendTransactionConfig.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSendTransactionConfig")
\>, timeout: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[Timeout](../types/types/struct.Timeout.html "struct helius::types::types::Timeout")
\>, ) -> [Result](../error/type.Result.html "type helius::error::Result")
<[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
\>

Sends a smart transaction using seed bytes

This method allows for sending smart transactions in asynchronous contexts where the Signer trait’s lack of Send + Sync would otherwise cause issues. It creates Keypairs from the provided seed bytes and uses them to sign the transaction.

##### [§](#arguments-19)
Arguments

*   `create_config` - A `CreateSmartTransactionSeedConfig` containing:
    *   `instructions`: The instructions to be executed in the transaction.
    *   `signer_seeds`: Seed bytes for generating signer keypairs.
    *   `fee_payer_seed`: Optional seed bytes for generating the fee payer keypair.
    *   `lookup_tables`: Optional address lookup tables for the transaction.
*   `send_options` - Optional `RpcSendTransactionConfig` for sending the transaction.
*   `timeout` - Optional `Timeout` wait time for polling transaction confirmation.

##### [§](#returns-22)
Returns

A `Result<Signature>` containing the transaction signature if successful, or an error if not.

##### [§](#errors)
Errors

This function will return an error if keypair creation from seeds fails, the transaction sending fails, or no signer seeds are provided

##### [§](#notes)
Notes

If no `fee_payer_seed` is provided, the first signer (i.e., derived from the first seed in `signer_seeds`) will be used as the fee payer

#### fn [into\_either](https://docs.rs/either/1.13.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/either/into_either/trait.IntoEither.html#method.into_either)
(self, into\_left: [bool](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.bool.html)
) -> [Either](https://docs.rs/either/1.13.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/either/enum.Either.html "enum either::Either")
<Self, Self>

Converts `self` into a [`Left`](https://docs.rs/either/1.13.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/either/enum.Either.html#variant.Left "variant either::Either::Left")
 variant of [`Either<Self, Self>`](https://docs.rs/either/1.13.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/either/enum.Either.html "enum either::Either")
 if `into_left` is `true`. Converts `self` into a [`Right`](https://docs.rs/either/1.13.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/either/enum.Either.html#variant.Right "variant either::Either::Right")
 variant of [`Either<Self, Self>`](https://docs.rs/either/1.13.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/either/enum.Either.html "enum either::Either")
 otherwise. [Read more](https://docs.rs/either/1.13.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/either/into_either/trait.IntoEither.html#method.into_either)

[Source](https://docs.rs/either/1.13.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/either/into_either.rs.html#55-57)

,

Converts `self` into a [`Left`](https://docs.rs/either/1.13.0/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/either/enum.Either.html#variant.Left "variant either::Either::Left")

#### helius's sandbox limits

All the builds on docs.rs are executed inside a sandbox with limited resources. The limits for this crate are the following:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Available RAM | 6.44 GB |
| Maximum rustdoc execution time | 15 minutes |
| Maximum size of a build log | 102.40 kB |
| Network access | blocked |
| Maximum number of build targets | 10  |

If a build fails because it hit one of those limits please [open an issue](https://github.com/rust-lang/docs.rs/issues/new/choose)
 to get them increased.

Struct HeliusAsyncSolanaClientCopy item path
============================================

[Source](../../src/helius/client.rs.html#179-181)

    pub struct HeliusAsyncSolanaClient { /* private fields */ }

Expand description

A wrapper around the asynchronous Solana RPC client that provides thread-safe access

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#527)

#### pub fn [commitment](#method.commitment)
(&self) -> [CommitmentConfig](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/commitment_config/struct.CommitmentConfig.html "struct solana_sdk::commitment_config::CommitmentConfig")

Get the configured default [commitment level](https://solana.com/docs/rpc#configuring-state-commitment)
.

The commitment config may be specified during construction, and determines how thoroughly committed a transaction must be when waiting for its confirmation or otherwise checking for confirmation. If not specified, the default commitment level is [`Finalized`](CommitmentLevel::Finalized)
.

The default commitment level is overridden when calling methods that explicitly provide a [`CommitmentConfig`](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/commitment_config/struct.CommitmentConfig.html "struct solana_sdk::commitment_config::CommitmentConfig")
, like [`RpcClient::confirm_transaction_with_commitment`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.confirm_transaction_with_commitment "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::confirm_transaction_with_commitment")
.

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#592-595)

#### pub async fn [send\_and\_confirm\_transaction](#method.send_and_confirm_transaction)
( &self, transaction: &impl [SerializableTransaction](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/rpc_client/trait.SerializableTransaction.html "trait solana_rpc_client::rpc_client::SerializableTransaction")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Submit a transaction and wait for confirmation.

Once this function returns successfully, the given transaction is guaranteed to be processed with the configured [commitment level](https://solana.com/docs/rpc#configuring-state-commitment)
.

After sending the transaction, this method polls in a loop for the status of the transaction until it has ben confirmed.

##### [§](#errors)
Errors

If the transaction is not signed then an error with kind [`RpcError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html "enum solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError")
 is returned, containing an [`RpcResponseError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html#variant.RpcResponseError "variant solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError::RpcResponseError")
 with `code` set to [`JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_TRANSACTION_SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILURE`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/custom_error/constant.JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_TRANSACTION_SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILURE.html "constant solana_rpc_client_api::custom_error::JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_TRANSACTION_SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILURE")
.

If the preflight transaction simulation fails then an error with kind [`RpcError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html "enum solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError")
 is returned, containing an [`RpcResponseError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html#variant.RpcResponseError "variant solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError::RpcResponseError")
 with `code` set to [`JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_SEND_TRANSACTION_PREFLIGHT_FAILURE`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/custom_error/constant.JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_SEND_TRANSACTION_PREFLIGHT_FAILURE.html "constant solana_rpc_client_api::custom_error::JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_SEND_TRANSACTION_PREFLIGHT_FAILURE")
.

If the receiving node is unhealthy, e.g. it is not fully synced to the cluster, then an error with kind [`RpcError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html "enum solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError")
 is returned, containing an [`RpcResponseError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html#variant.RpcResponseError "variant solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError::RpcResponseError")
 with `code` set to [`JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_NODE_UNHEALTHY`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/custom_error/constant.JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_NODE_UNHEALTHY.html "constant solana_rpc_client_api::custom_error::JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_NODE_UNHEALTHY")
.

##### [§](#rpc-reference)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`sendTransaction`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/sendtransaction)
 RPC method, and the [`getLatestBlockhash`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getlatestblockhash)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples)
Examples

    let tx = system_transaction::transfer(&alice, &bob.pubkey(), lamports, latest_blockhash);
    let signature = rpc_client.send_and_confirm_transaction(&tx).await?;

( &self, transaction: &impl [SerializableTransaction](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/rpc_client/trait.SerializableTransaction.html "trait solana_rpc_client::rpc_client::SerializableTransaction")

#### pub async fn [send\_transaction](#method.send_transaction)
( &self, transaction: &impl [SerializableTransaction](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/rpc_client/trait.SerializableTransaction.html "trait solana_rpc_client::rpc_client::SerializableTransaction")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Submits a signed transaction to the network.

Before a transaction is processed, the receiving node runs a “preflight check” which verifies signatures, checks that the node is healthy, and simulates the transaction. If the preflight check fails then an error is returned immediately. Preflight checks can be disabled by calling [`send_transaction_with_config`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.send_transaction_with_config "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::send_transaction_with_config")
 and setting the [`skip_preflight`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSendTransactionConfig.html#structfield.skip_preflight "field solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSendTransactionConfig::skip_preflight")
 field of [`RpcSendTransactionConfig`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSendTransactionConfig.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSendTransactionConfig")
 to `true`.

This method does not wait for the transaction to be processed or confirmed before returning successfully. To wait for the transaction to be processed or confirmed, use the [`send_and_confirm_transaction`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.send_and_confirm_transaction "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::send_and_confirm_transaction")
 method.

##### [§](#errors-1)
Errors

If the transaction is not signed then an error with kind [`RpcError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html "enum solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError")
 is returned, containing an [`RpcResponseError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html#variant.RpcResponseError "variant solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError::RpcResponseError")
 with `code` set to [`JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_TRANSACTION_SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILURE`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/custom_error/constant.JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_TRANSACTION_SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILURE.html "constant solana_rpc_client_api::custom_error::JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_TRANSACTION_SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILURE")
.

If the preflight transaction simulation fails then an error with kind [`RpcError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html "enum solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError")
 is returned, containing an [`RpcResponseError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html#variant.RpcResponseError "variant solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError::RpcResponseError")
 with `code` set to [`JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_SEND_TRANSACTION_PREFLIGHT_FAILURE`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/custom_error/constant.JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_SEND_TRANSACTION_PREFLIGHT_FAILURE.html "constant solana_rpc_client_api::custom_error::JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_SEND_TRANSACTION_PREFLIGHT_FAILURE")
.

If the receiving node is unhealthy, e.g. it is not fully synced to the cluster, then an error with kind [`RpcError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html "enum solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError")
 is returned, containing an [`RpcResponseError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html#variant.RpcResponseError "variant solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError::RpcResponseError")
 with `code` set to [`JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_NODE_UNHEALTHY`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/custom_error/constant.JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_NODE_UNHEALTHY.html "constant solana_rpc_client_api::custom_error::JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_NODE_UNHEALTHY")
.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-1)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`sendTransaction`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/sendtransaction)
 RPC method.

    let latest_blockhash = rpc_client.get_latest_blockhash().await?;
    let tx = system_transaction::transfer(&alice, &bob.pubkey(), lamports, latest_blockhash);
    let signature = rpc_client.send_transaction(&tx).await?;

#### pub async fn [send\_transaction\_with\_config](#method.send_transaction_with_config)
( &self, transaction: &impl [SerializableTransaction](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/rpc_client/trait.SerializableTransaction.html "trait solana_rpc_client::rpc_client::SerializableTransaction")
, config: [RpcSendTransactionConfig](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSendTransactionConfig.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSendTransactionConfig")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Submits a signed transaction to the network.

Before a transaction is processed, the receiving node runs a “preflight check” which verifies signatures, checks that the node is healthy, and simulates the transaction. If the preflight check fails then an error is returned immediately. Preflight checks can be disabled by setting the [`skip_preflight`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSendTransactionConfig.html#structfield.skip_preflight "field solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSendTransactionConfig::skip_preflight")
 field of [`RpcSendTransactionConfig`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSendTransactionConfig.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSendTransactionConfig")
 to `true`.

This method does not wait for the transaction to be processed or confirmed before returning successfully. To wait for the transaction to be processed or confirmed, use the [`send_and_confirm_transaction`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.send_and_confirm_transaction "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::send_and_confirm_transaction")
 method.

##### [§](#errors-2)
Errors

If preflight checks are enabled, if the transaction is not signed then an error with kind [`RpcError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html "enum solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError")
 is returned, containing an [`RpcResponseError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html#variant.RpcResponseError "variant solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError::RpcResponseError")
 with `code` set to [`JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_TRANSACTION_SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILURE`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/custom_error/constant.JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_TRANSACTION_SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILURE.html "constant solana_rpc_client_api::custom_error::JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_TRANSACTION_SIGNATURE_VERIFICATION_FAILURE")
.

If preflight checks are enabled, if the preflight transaction simulation fails then an error with kind [`RpcError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html "enum solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError")
 is returned, containing an [`RpcResponseError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html#variant.RpcResponseError "variant solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError::RpcResponseError")
 with `code` set to [`JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_SEND_TRANSACTION_PREFLIGHT_FAILURE`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/custom_error/constant.JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_SEND_TRANSACTION_PREFLIGHT_FAILURE.html "constant solana_rpc_client_api::custom_error::JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_SEND_TRANSACTION_PREFLIGHT_FAILURE")
.

If the receiving node is unhealthy, e.g. it is not fully synced to the cluster, then an error with kind [`RpcError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html "enum solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError")
 is returned, containing an [`RpcResponseError`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/request/enum.RpcError.html#variant.RpcResponseError "variant solana_rpc_client_api::request::RpcError::RpcResponseError")
 with `code` set to [`JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_NODE_UNHEALTHY`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/custom_error/constant.JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_NODE_UNHEALTHY.html "constant solana_rpc_client_api::custom_error::JSON_RPC_SERVER_ERROR_NODE_UNHEALTHY")
.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-2)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`sendTransaction`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/sendtransaction)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-2)
Examples

    // Transfer lamports from Alice to Bob
    let latest_blockhash = rpc_client.get_latest_blockhash().await?;
    let tx = system_transaction::transfer(&alice, &bob.pubkey(), lamports, latest_blockhash);
    let config = RpcSendTransactionConfig {
        skip_preflight: true,
        .. RpcSendTransactionConfig::default()
    };
    let signature = rpc_client.send_transaction_with_config(
        &tx,
        config,
    ).await?;

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#979)

#### pub async fn [confirm\_transaction](#method.confirm_transaction)
( &self, signature: &[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[bool](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.bool.html)
, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Check the confirmation status of a transaction.

Returns `true` if the given transaction succeeded and has been committed with the configured [commitment level](https://solana.com/docs/rpc#configuring-state-commitment)
, which can be retrieved with the [`commitment`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.commitment "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::commitment")
 method.

Note that this method does not wait for a transaction to be confirmed — it only checks whether a transaction has been confirmed. To submit a transaction and wait for it to confirm, use [`send_and_confirm_transaction`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.send_and_confirm_transaction "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::send_and_confirm_transaction")
.

_This method returns `false` if the transaction failed, even if it has been confirmed._

##### [§](#rpc-reference-3)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`getSignatureStatuses`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getsignaturestatuses)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-3)
Examples

    // Transfer lamports from Alice to Bob and wait for confirmation
    let latest_blockhash = rpc_client.get_latest_blockhash().await?;
    let tx = system_transaction::transfer(&alice, &bob.pubkey(), lamports, latest_blockhash);
    let signature = rpc_client.send_transaction(&tx).await?;
    
    loop {
        let confirmed = rpc_client.confirm_transaction(&signature).await?;
        if confirmed {
            break;
        }
    }

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#1041-1045)

#### pub async fn [confirm\_transaction\_with\_commitment](#method.confirm_transaction_with_commitment)
( &self, signature: &[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
, commitment\_config: [CommitmentConfig](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/commitment_config/struct.CommitmentConfig.html "struct solana_sdk::commitment_config::CommitmentConfig")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Response](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.Response.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::Response")
<[bool](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.bool.html)
\>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Check the confirmation status of a transaction.

Returns an [`RpcResult`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/type.RpcResult.html "type solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcResult")
 with value `true` if the given transaction succeeded and has been committed with the given [commitment level](https://solana.com/docs/rpc#configuring-state-commitment)
.

Note that this method does not wait for a transaction to be confirmed — it only checks whether a transaction has been confirmed. To submit a transaction and wait for it to confirm, use [`send_and_confirm_transaction`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.send_and_confirm_transaction "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::send_and_confirm_transaction")
.

_This method returns an [`RpcResult`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/type.RpcResult.html "type solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcResult")
 with value `false` if the transaction failed, even if it has been confirmed._

##### [§](#rpc-reference-4)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`getSignatureStatuses`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getsignaturestatuses)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-4)
Examples

    // Transfer lamports from Alice to Bob and wait for confirmation
    let latest_blockhash = rpc_client.get_latest_blockhash().await?;
    let tx = system_transaction::transfer(&alice, &bob.pubkey(), lamports, latest_blockhash);
    let signature = rpc_client.send_transaction(&tx).await?;
    
    loop {
        let commitment_config = CommitmentConfig::processed();
        let confirmed = rpc_client.confirm_transaction_with_commitment(&signature, commitment_config).await?;
        if confirmed.value {
            break;
        }
    }

#### pub async fn [simulate\_transaction](#method.simulate_transaction)
( &self, transaction: &impl [SerializableTransaction](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/rpc_client/trait.SerializableTransaction.html "trait solana_rpc_client::rpc_client::SerializableTransaction")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Response](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.Response.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::Response")
<[RpcSimulateTransactionResult](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionResult.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSimulateTransactionResult")
\>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Simulates sending a transaction.

If the transaction fails, then the [`err`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionResult.html#structfield.err "field solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSimulateTransactionResult::err")
 field of the returned [`RpcSimulateTransactionResult`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionResult.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSimulateTransactionResult")
 will be `Some`. Any logs emitted from the transaction are returned in the [`logs`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionResult.html#structfield.logs "field solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSimulateTransactionResult::logs")
 field.

Simulating a transaction is similar to the [“preflight check”](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/sendtransaction)
 that is run by default when sending a transaction.

By default, signatures are not verified during simulation. To verify signatures, call the [`simulate_transaction_with_config`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.simulate_transaction_with_config "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::simulate_transaction_with_config")
 method, with the [`sig_verify`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionConfig.html#structfield.sig_verify "field solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSimulateTransactionConfig::sig_verify")
 field of [`RpcSimulateTransactionConfig`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionConfig.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSimulateTransactionConfig")
 set to `true`.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-5)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`simulateTransaction`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/simulatetransaction)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-5)
Examples

    // Transfer lamports from Alice to Bob
    let latest_blockhash = rpc_client.get_latest_blockhash().await?;
    let tx = system_transaction::transfer(&alice, &bob.pubkey(), lamports, latest_blockhash);
    let result = rpc_client.simulate_transaction(&tx).await?;
    assert!(result.value.err.is_none());

#### pub async fn [simulate\_transaction\_with\_config](#method.simulate_transaction_with_config)
( &self, transaction: &impl [SerializableTransaction](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/rpc_client/trait.SerializableTransaction.html "trait solana_rpc_client::rpc_client::SerializableTransaction")

\>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Simulates sending a transaction.

If the transaction fails, then the [`err`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionResult.html#structfield.err "field solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSimulateTransactionResult::err")
 field of the returned [`RpcSimulateTransactionResult`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionResult.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSimulateTransactionResult")
 will be `Some`. Any logs emitted from the transaction are returned in the [`logs`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionResult.html#structfield.logs "field solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSimulateTransactionResult::logs")
 field.

Simulating a transaction is similar to the [“preflight check”](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/sendtransaction)
 that is run by default when sending a transaction.

By default, signatures are not verified during simulation. To verify signatures, call the [`simulate_transaction_with_config`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.simulate_transaction_with_config "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::simulate_transaction_with_config")

 set to `true`.

This method can additionally query information about accounts by including them in the [`accounts`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionConfig.html#structfield.accounts "field solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSimulateTransactionConfig::accounts")
 field of the [`RpcSimulateTransactionConfig`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/config/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionConfig.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::config::RpcSimulateTransactionConfig")
 argument, in which case those results are reported in the [`accounts`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionResult.html#structfield.accounts "field solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSimulateTransactionResult::accounts")
 field of the returned [`RpcSimulateTransactionResult`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSimulateTransactionResult.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSimulateTransactionResult")
.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-6)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`simulateTransaction`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/simulatetransaction)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-6)
Examples

    // Transfer lamports from Alice to Bob
    let latest_blockhash = rpc_client.get_latest_blockhash().await?;
    let tx = system_transaction::transfer(&alice, &bob.pubkey(), lamports, latest_blockhash);
    let config = RpcSimulateTransactionConfig {
        sig_verify: true,
        .. RpcSimulateTransactionConfig::default()
    };

        &tx,

    ).await?;

#### pub async fn [get\_highest\_snapshot\_slot](#method.get_highest_snapshot_slot)
( &self, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[RpcSnapshotSlotInfo](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcSnapshotSlotInfo.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcSnapshotSlotInfo")

\>

This will find the highest full snapshot slot, and the highest incremental snapshot slot _based on_ the full snapshot slot, if there is one.

#### pub async fn [get\_signature\_status](#method.get_signature_status)
( &self, signature: &[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[()](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.unit.html)
, [TransactionError](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-error/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_error/enum.TransactionError.html "enum solana_transaction_error::TransactionError")
\>>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Check if a transaction has been processed with the default [commitment level](https://solana.com/docs/rpc#configuring-state-commitment)
.

If the transaction has been processed with the default commitment level, then this method returns `Ok` of `Some`. If the transaction has not yet been processed with the default commitment level, it returns `Ok` of `None`.

If the transaction has been processed with the default commitment level, and the transaction succeeded, this method returns `Ok(Some(Ok(())))`. If the transaction has been processed with the default commitment level, and the transaction failed, this method returns `Ok(Some(Err(_)))`, where the interior error is type [`TransactionError`](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-error/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_error/enum.TransactionError.html "enum solana_transaction_error::TransactionError")
.

This function only searches a node’s recent history, including all recent slots, plus up to [`MAX_RECENT_BLOCKHASHES`](https://docs.rs/solana-clock/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_clock/constant.MAX_RECENT_BLOCKHASHES.html "constant solana_clock::MAX_RECENT_BLOCKHASHES")
 rooted slots. To search the full transaction history use the [`get_signature_status_with_commitment_and_history`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.get_signature_status_with_commitment_and_history "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::get_signature_status_with_commitment_and_history")
 method.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-8)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`getSignatureStatuses`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getsignaturestatuses)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-8)
Examples

    let signature = rpc_client.send_transaction(&tx).await?;
    let status = rpc_client.get_signature_status(&signature).await?;

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#1478-1481)

#### pub async fn [get\_signature\_statuses](#method.get_signature_statuses)
( &self, signatures: &\[[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")\
\], ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Response](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.Response.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::Response")
<[Vec](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/vec/struct.Vec.html "struct alloc::vec::Vec")
<[Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[TransactionStatus](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-status-client-types/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_status_client_types/struct.TransactionStatus.html "struct solana_transaction_status_client_types::TransactionStatus")
\>>>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Gets the statuses of a list of transaction signatures.

The returned vector of [`TransactionStatus`](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-status-client-types/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_status_client_types/struct.TransactionStatus.html "struct solana_transaction_status_client_types::TransactionStatus")
 has the same length as the input slice.

For any transaction that has not been processed by the network, the value of the corresponding entry in the returned vector is `None`. As a result, a transaction that has recently been submitted will not have a status immediately.

To submit a transaction and wait for it to confirm, use [`send_and_confirm_transaction`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.send_and_confirm_transaction "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::send_and_confirm_transaction")
.

This function ignores the configured confirmation level, and returns the transaction status whatever it is. It does not wait for transactions to be processed.

This function only searches a node’s recent history, including all recent slots, plus up to [`MAX_RECENT_BLOCKHASHES`](https://docs.rs/solana-clock/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_clock/constant.MAX_RECENT_BLOCKHASHES.html "constant solana_clock::MAX_RECENT_BLOCKHASHES")
 rooted slots. To search the full transaction history use the [`get_signature_statuses_with_history`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.get_signature_statuses_with_history "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::get_signature_statuses_with_history")
 method.

##### [§](#errors-3)
Errors

Any individual `TransactionStatus` may have triggered an error during processing, in which case its [`err`](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-status-client-types/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_status_client_types/struct.TransactionStatus.html#structfield.err "field solana_transaction_status_client_types::TransactionStatus::err")
 field will be `Some`.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-9)
RPC Reference

This method corresponds directly to the [`getSignatureStatuses`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getsignaturestatuses)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-9)
Examples

    // Send lamports from Alice to Bob and wait for the transaction to be processed
    let latest_blockhash = rpc_client.get_latest_blockhash().await?;
    let tx = system_transaction::transfer(&alice, &bob.pubkey(), lamports, latest_blockhash);
    let signature = rpc_client.send_transaction(&tx).await?;
    
    let status = loop {
       let statuses = rpc_client.get_signature_statuses(&[signature]).await?.value;
       if let Some(status) = statuses[0].clone() {
           break status;
       }
       std::thread::sleep(Duration::from_millis(100));
    };
    
    assert!(status.err.is_none());

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#1549-1552)

#### pub async fn [get\_signature\_statuses\_with\_history](#method.get_signature_statuses_with_history)
( &self, signatures: &\[[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")\
\], ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Response](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.Response.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::Response")
<[Vec](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/vec/struct.Vec.html "struct alloc::vec::Vec")
<[Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[TransactionStatus](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-status-client-types/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_status_client_types/struct.TransactionStatus.html "struct solana_transaction_status_client_types::TransactionStatus")
\>>>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Gets the statuses of a list of transaction signatures.

The returned vector of [`TransactionStatus`](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-status-client-types/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_status_client_types/struct.TransactionStatus.html "struct solana_transaction_status_client_types::TransactionStatus")
 has the same length as the input slice.

For any transaction that has not been processed by the network, the value of the corresponding entry in the returned vector is `None`. As a result, a transaction that has recently been submitted will not have a status immediately.

To submit a transaction and wait for it to confirm, use [`send_and_confirm_transaction`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.send_and_confirm_transaction "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::send_and_confirm_transaction")
.

This function ignores the configured confirmation level, and returns the transaction status whatever it is. It does not wait for transactions to be processed.

This function searches a node’s full ledger history and (if implemented) long-term storage. To search for transactions in recent slots only use the [`get_signature_statuses`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.get_signature_statuses "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::get_signature_statuses")
 method.

##### [§](#errors-4)
Errors

Any individual `TransactionStatus` may have triggered an error during processing, in which case its [`err`](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-status-client-types/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_status_client_types/struct.TransactionStatus.html#structfield.err "field solana_transaction_status_client_types::TransactionStatus::err")
 field will be `Some`.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-10)
RPC Reference

This method corresponds directly to the [`getSignatureStatuses`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getsignaturestatuses)
 RPC method, with the `searchTransactionHistory` configuration option set to `true`.

##### [§](#examples-10)
Examples

    // Check if an old transaction exists
    let signature = get_old_transaction_signature();
    let latest_blockhash = rpc_client.get_latest_blockhash().await?;
    let statuses = rpc_client.get_signature_statuses_with_history(&[signature]).await?.value;
    if statuses[0].is_none() {
        println!("old transaction does not exist");
    }

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#1622-1626)

#### pub async fn [get\_signature\_status\_with\_commitment](#method.get_signature_status_with_commitment)
( &self, signature: &[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
, commitment\_config: [CommitmentConfig](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/commitment_config/struct.CommitmentConfig.html "struct solana_sdk::commitment_config::CommitmentConfig")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[()](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.unit.html)
, [TransactionError](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-error/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_error/enum.TransactionError.html "enum solana_transaction_error::TransactionError")
\>>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Check if a transaction has been processed with the given [commitment level](https://solana.com/docs/rpc#configuring-state-commitment)
.

If the transaction has been processed with the given commitment level, then this method returns `Ok` of `Some`. If the transaction has not yet been processed with the given commitment level, it returns `Ok` of `None`.

If the transaction has been processed with the given commitment level, and the transaction succeeded, this method returns `Ok(Some(Ok(())))`. If the transaction has been processed with the given commitment level, and the transaction failed, this method returns `Ok(Some(Err(_)))`, where the interior error is type [`TransactionError`](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-error/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_error/enum.TransactionError.html "enum solana_transaction_error::TransactionError")
.

This function only searches a node’s recent history, including all recent slots, plus up to [`MAX_RECENT_BLOCKHASHES`](https://docs.rs/solana-clock/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_clock/constant.MAX_RECENT_BLOCKHASHES.html "constant solana_clock::MAX_RECENT_BLOCKHASHES")
 rooted slots. To search the full transaction history use the [`get_signature_status_with_commitment_and_history`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.get_signature_status_with_commitment_and_history "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::get_signature_status_with_commitment_and_history")
 method.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-11)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`getSignatureStatuses`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getsignaturestatuses)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-11)
Examples

    let signature = rpc_client.send_and_confirm_transaction(&tx).await?;
    let commitment_config = CommitmentConfig::processed();
    let status = rpc_client.get_signature_status_with_commitment(
        &signature,
        commitment_config,
    ).await?;

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#1696-1701)

#### pub async fn [get\_signature\_status\_with\_commitment\_and\_history](#method.get_signature_status_with_commitment_and_history)
( &self, signature: &[Signature](https://docs.rs/solana-signature/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_signature/struct.Signature.html "struct solana_signature::Signature")
, commitment\_config: [CommitmentConfig](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/commitment_config/struct.CommitmentConfig.html "struct solana_sdk::commitment_config::CommitmentConfig")
, search\_transaction\_history: [bool](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.bool.html)
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[()](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.unit.html)
, [TransactionError](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-error/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_error/enum.TransactionError.html "enum solana_transaction_error::TransactionError")
\>>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Check if a transaction has been processed with the given [commitment level](https://solana.com/docs/rpc#configuring-state-commitment)
.

If the transaction has been processed with the given commitment level, then this method returns `Ok` of `Some`. If the transaction has not yet been processed with the given commitment level, it returns `Ok` of `None`.

If the transaction has been processed with the given commitment level, and the transaction succeeded, this method returns `Ok(Some(Ok(())))`. If the transaction has been processed with the given commitment level, and the transaction failed, this method returns `Ok(Some(Err(_)))`, where the interior error is type [`TransactionError`](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-error/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_error/enum.TransactionError.html "enum solana_transaction_error::TransactionError")
.

This method optionally searches a node’s full ledger history and (if implemented) long-term storage.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-12)
RPC Reference

This method is built on the [`getSignatureStatuses`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getsignaturestatuses)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-12)
Examples

    let signature = rpc_client.send_transaction(&tx).await?;
    let commitment_config = CommitmentConfig::processed();
    let search_transaction_history = true;

        &signature,
        commitment_config,
        search_transaction_history,
    ).await?;

#### pub async fn [get\_block](#method.get_block)
(&self, slot: [u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[EncodedConfirmedBlock](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-status-client-types/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_status_client_types/struct.EncodedConfirmedBlock.html "struct solana_transaction_status_client_types::EncodedConfirmedBlock")
, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Returns identity and transaction information about a confirmed block in the ledger.

The encodings are returned in [`UiTransactionEncoding::Json`](https://docs.rs/solana-transaction-status-client-types/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_transaction_status_client_types/enum.UiTransactionEncoding.html#variant.Json "variant solana_transaction_status_client_types::UiTransactionEncoding::Json")
 format. To return transactions in other encodings, use [`get_block_with_encoding`](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client/struct.RpcClient.html#method.get_block_with_encoding "method solana_rpc_client::nonblocking::rpc_client::RpcClient::get_block_with_encoding")
.

#### pub async fn [get\_blocks](#method.get_blocks)
( &self, start\_slot: [u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
, end\_slot: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
\>, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Vec](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/vec/struct.Vec.html "struct alloc::vec::Vec")
<[u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
\>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Returns a list of finalized blocks between two slots.

The range is inclusive, with results including the block for both `start_slot` and `end_slot`.

If `end_slot` is not provided, then the end slot is for the latest finalized block.

This method may not return blocks for the full range of slots if some slots do not have corresponding blocks. To simply get a specific number of sequential blocks, use the [`get_blocks_with_limit`](RpcClient::get_blocks_with_limit.)
 method.

This method uses the [`Finalized`](CommitmentLevel::Finalized)
 [commitment level](https://solana.com/docs/rpc#configuring-state-commitment)
.

##### [§](#errors-5)
Errors

This method returns an error if the range is greater than 500,000 slots.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-30)
RPC Reference

This method corresponds directly to the [`getBlocks`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getblocks)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-30)
Examples

    // Get up to the first 10 blocks
    let start_slot = 0;
    let end_slot = 9;
    let blocks = rpc_client.get_blocks(start_slot, Some(end_slot)).await?;

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#2493-2498)

#### pub async fn [get\_blocks\_with\_commitment](#method.get_blocks_with_commitment)
( &self, start\_slot: [u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
, end\_slot: [Option](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/option/enum.Option.html "enum core::option::Option")
<[u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
\>, commitment\_config: [CommitmentConfig](https://docs.rs/solana-sdk/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_sdk/commitment_config/struct.CommitmentConfig.html "struct solana_sdk::commitment_config::CommitmentConfig")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")
<[Vec](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/alloc/vec/struct.Vec.html "struct alloc::vec::Vec")
<[u64](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/std/primitive.u64.html)
\>, [Error](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/client_error/struct.Error.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::client_error::Error")
\>

Returns a list of confirmed blocks between two slots.

The range is inclusive, with results including the block for both `start_slot` and `end_slot`.

If `end_slot` is not provided, then the end slot is for the latest block with the given [commitment level](https://solana.com/docs/rpc#configuring-state-commitment)
.

This method may not return blocks for the full range of slots if some slots do not have corresponding blocks. To simply get a specific number of sequential blocks, use the [`get_blocks_with_limit_and_commitment`](RpcClient::get_blocks_with_limit_and_commitment.)
 method.

##### [§](#errors-6)
Errors

This method returns an error if the range is greater than 500,000 slots.

This method returns an error if the given commitment level is below [`Confirmed`](CommitmentLevel::Confirmed)
.

##### [§](#rpc-reference-31)
RPC Reference

This method corresponds directly to the [`getBlocks`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getblocks)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-31)
Examples

    // Get up to the first 10 blocks
    let start_slot = 0;
    let end_slot = 9;
    // Method does not support commitment below `confirmed`
    let commitment_config = CommitmentConfig::confirmed();
    let blocks = rpc_client.get_blocks_with_commitment(
        start_slot,
        Some(end_slot),
        commitment_config,
    ).await?;

[Source](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/src/solana_rpc_client/nonblocking/rpc_client.rs.html#2540-2544)

#### pub async fn [get\_signatures\_for\_address](#method.get_signatures_for_address)
( &self, address: &[Pubkey](https://docs.rs/solana-pubkey/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_pubkey/struct.Pubkey.html "struct solana_pubkey::Pubkey")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")

<[RpcConfirmedTransactionStatusWithSignature](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client-api/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client_api/response/struct.RpcConfirmedTransactionStatusWithSignature.html "struct solana_rpc_client_api::response::RpcConfirmedTransactionStatusWithSignature")

#### pub async fn [get\_signatures\_for\_address\_with\_config](#method.get_signatures_for_address_with_config)
( &self, address: &[Pubkey](https://docs.rs/solana-pubkey/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_pubkey/struct.Pubkey.html "struct solana_pubkey::Pubkey")
, config: [GetConfirmedSignaturesForAddress2Config](https://docs.rs/solana-rpc-client/2.1.4/x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/solana_rpc_client/rpc_client/struct.GetConfirmedSignaturesForAddress2Config.html "struct solana_rpc_client::rpc_client::GetConfirmedSignaturesForAddress2Config")
, ) -> [Result](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/core/result/enum.Result.html "enum core::result::Result")

##### [§](#errors-9)

##### [§](#rpc-reference-35)

This method corresponds directly to the [`getSignaturesForAddress`](https://solana.com/docs/rpc/http/getsignaturesforaddress)
 RPC method.

##### [§](#examples-35)
Examples

    let config = GetConfirmedSignaturesForAddress2Config {
        before: None,
        until: None,
        limit: Some(3),
        commitment: Some(CommitmentConfig::confirmed()),
    };
    let signatures = rpc_client.get_signatures_for_address_with_config(
        &alice.pubkey(),
        config,
    ).await?;
